 )(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) hard discs kaa data ricover karne ke kai tareeke hai
 These days, the reason of cloud storage is less in the trend of external hard disk
 lekin phir bhi external hard drive yuj kiye jate hai
 There is always a problem of data loss with hard drives
 kabhi hard discs krash kar jaati he to kabhi virus yaa mailaware kii vajah se data yuj karne main dikkat hoti he
 Your computer does not detect hard disks due to viruses and because of this you need a format
 kai baar galati se bhi data delit ho jaataa he
 In such a situation you always have the option to recover data
 hard discs se data ricover karne kaa ye tarika tab hi kaam karegaa jab hard discs aapke computer main detect ho rahaa he
 Many times due to a hardware problem, the hard disk in the computer does not detect itself, in which case it is also difficult to recover
 hard discs ricover karne ke liye internet par kaisoftwareya tuls mil jaaenge
 Many of these tools are also premium, which you pay for and take their full subscription
 ham aapako ek aisa tarika bataate hai jiske jariye aap bina kisi software ke external hard discs kaa data ricover kar sakate hai
 It is not that 100% of your data will be recovered in this way
 kyonki kai baar ye tarika kaam nahin karata he
 But you can try it
 iske alaava kuch credibal software ke bare main bhi bataate hai
 That is, if it does not do tricks without software, then you can resort to software
 pehla tarika (ye tarika Windows computer ke liye he, mike ke liye nahin)--- hard drive ko apane computer se cabel ke jariye conect karen
 Type CMD by pressing Windows + r and open Command Prompt
 --- apane external hard drive kaa Drive Letter check karen
 Generally it is f or G
 kyonki inbilt hard drive ke letters shuruaati hote hai jaise C, d or E
 --- Now type this at Command Prompt ATTRIB -H -R -S / s / DH: *
 * (ATTRIB ke baad pehla letters aapke external hard drive kaa letters hago jo yahaan –H he)--- enter press karte hi file ricover kaa process shuru hota he
 It takes some time and files are recovered
 jaisaa kii hamane pehle bhi bataaya he ki ye tarika kai baak kuch technical vajahon se kaam nahin karata he
 Open Command Prompt from Run As Administrator
 software ke jarieinternet par kai software hai jinamein Easeus or Recuva popular hai
 Through them you can recover files
 haalanki inke kuch fitures locd yaa premium hote hai jinhen yuj karne ke liye aapako inaki sabsakripshan leni hogi

 In the case of government pension or other benefits, it cannot be said that these benefits will not be available because you do not have an Aadhaar card, but if there is a case of income tax or other non-beneficial cases, then the government can ask for Aadhaar card and the government stopped Can not go haalanki CJI khehar ne kaha tha ki maamla samvidhan peeth ke paas he, lekin philhal is maamle kii sunwaayee nahin karenge
 This is in violation of the orders of the Supreme Court
 ye logon ke rhite tu privesi ke khilaaf he
 Anyway, there is already a provision of PAN card for income tax and in such a situation it is not necessary to make Aadhaar card mandatory
 sarkaar ne pehle aadhaar ko mani bill ke taur par paas kiya jo khud hi manamaana or ansavaidhanik he
 However, a few days ago the Supreme Court had said that the Constitution Bench has already ordered that if there is a case for a beneficial scheme then the Aadhar card cannot be made mandatory
 sarkaar pension yaa duusare laabh dene ke maamle main ye nahin kaha ja saktaa ki ye laabh nahin milenge kyonki aapke paas aadhaar card nahin he, lekin agar inakam tex yaa duusare naan benificial maamalon kaa maamla he to sarkaar aadhaar card maang sakati he or sarkaar ko roka nahin ja saktaa
 Although CJI Khehar had said that the matter is with the Constitution Bench, but will not hear the matter at present
 saal 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaav main abhi vakt he, magar bihar main rajnatik uthapatak chaalu he
 But in the formula that is being given for the next Lok Sabha elections, BJP will contest 20 seats whereas BJP has 22 mps
 jediu 12 siton par chunaav ladegi jiske paas 2 saansad hai
 JDU may be given another seat in Jharkhand or Uttar Pradesh
 ramvilas paswan paanch seat ladenge jinke paas chah saansad hai jabaki kushvaha ko do siten di gai he jinke abhi teen saansad hai
 Obviously, there was bound to be a split on this partition
 is bantwaare se sabase adhik ghate main hai upendra kushvaha, jo maanav sansaadhan mantralay main rajyamantri hai or jisase ve santusht nahin hai
 At the same time, BJP is giving its support to a rebel MP of his party, which has made Kushwaha more angry
 ramvilas paswan pichhali baar saat siton par lade the chah siton par jite
 But this time he is sitting silent with five seats, because he is considered a meteorologist of politics
 unke chah saansadon main se teen ghar ke log hai, ek chota bhai or betaa
 In such a situation, his priority would be to win his clan
 agar ek saansad kii bali deni padi to ve iske liye taiyaar hai
 Nitish Kumar, who has only two mps, is not in any position to bargain with the BJP
 ek to unako apni sarkaar chalaani he bijepi ke sahare, doosraa kendra ke rahamokaram par bhi rahanaa he
 However, the Center has not even given the money of the announced package to Bihar, which has become a matter of losing credibility for Nitish Kumar
 duusare bijepi ne rajyasabha main jediu saansad ko upaadhyaksh banaaya or ab vah aisa dikhaa rahi he jaise usne nitish kumaar par ahsaan kiya ho
 In such a situation, Nitish Kumar will also consider it good to keep quiet
 bijepi 22 saansad hone ke baavjood 20 seat par lard rahi he
 Apparently he knows that the feedback from some of his mps is not good
 aise main use kuch saansadon ke tikat kaatane hi the
 Second, two of its mps, Kirti Azad and Shatrughan Sinha, have been rebel
 inkaa tikat to katnaa hi tha
 Now it has to be seen whether the BJP brings a second candidate to these seats or leaves it to the JDU
 ab waapas chalate hai uprendra kushvaha par, bijepi ne unhen do seat dekar kahin kaa nahin choda he
 Probably this will be foreseen to Kushwaha, so they have talked about cooking milk from Yaduvansha and rice from Kushvansha
 phir unhone kaha ki endie main kuch log modi ko dubaara pradhanmantri ke rup main nahin dekhnaa chaahate hai
 After all, what message does Kushwaha want to convey? unke paas tejasvi yadav kaa ofer pehle se hi he ki kushvaha ji kaa mahagathbandhan main swaagat he
 Kushwaha also knows that if they join the Grand Alliance, they will be in better shape of bargaining because if Yadav, Muslim, Manjhi's Sush Kushwaha joins, then the Mahagathbandhan will become a force that will give a tough fight to the NDA as their vote is 38 percent

 isse jo rajasav aayega, uskaa istemaal garibon, vanchiton or haashiye ke logon ke kalyaan ke liye kiya jayega
 There is a concern that recent developments will reverse your promise of maximum governance and minimum government
 aalochakon kaa kahana he ki notebandi ke baad sarkaar kii bhoomika or bad jaaegi
 This step will bring back the rule of income tax raids and you are relying more on the income tax officials, bankers and babus, while they are also the most corrupt
 is beemaari se nibatane ke liye aap kya kadam uthaaenge?pehle iskar ke adhikari andhere main tir chalaate the
 He would pick anyone up on his own accord, raid him anywhere at any time and you know what the result was usually
 aaj log khud aage aakar bainkon main apana paisa jamaa karvaa rahe hai
 This means that a financial identity has been established, no matter how much one tries to avoid it
 isaki padtaal technology sanchalit vaigyanik, paardarshee or vastunishth pranaaliyon ke madhyam se aasaani se kii ja sakati he
 Contrary to your question, demonetisation will actually end the will of the Income Tax authorities and give a direction to the war against corruption
 ise or aage le jaakar dekhen to isse kar prakriyaayein aasaan hongi or adhikari tathaa karadaata ke bich kaa rishta sahaj hoga
 The Department of Revenue is creating a system where the entire process of assessment will be online and the taxpayer will no longer need to appear before the officer
 ham aadhunik takneekon or praudyogiki kaa bhi zyada se zyada istemaal kar rahe hai, jaise big data analysis or data mining
 Through this, the selection of cases for investigation will be based on objective evidence and will not go according to the wishes of the authorities
 iskaa uddeshy yah he ki eemaandaar karadaata kaa utpeeda na hone paae or use takalif na ho, jabaki beyimaan kar chor ko pakad kar dandit kiya ja sake

 meri sarkaar bhrashtachar ko bilkul bardaasht nahin karegi

 isse nibatane ke liye aap kya upaay apana rahe hai?mujhe khushi he ki aapane yah sawaal poocha

 mujhe khushi he ki ab ve is baat ko sweekaar kar rahe hai ki nakadi kaa kaale dhan main bada haath hota he
 Demonetization was not a sudden move
 yah kai kadamon kii shrunkhlaa main ek kadam bhar he jo ham sarkaar banane ke baad se lagaataar uthaa rahe hai jinke tahat kaale dhan ke pravaah or bhandar par hamalaa kar rahe hai
 Some examples of this were the first decision of this government to form a Special Task Force on Black Money (SIT), the Foreign Black Money Act in 2015, mandating PAN, TCS of 1 per cent on all cash purchases above 2 lakhs (source Tax on taxes), excise duty on jewelery traders to make gold sales accountable and all information exchange and tax agreements with countries like Switzerland, Mauritius and Cyprus 
 notebandi ko lagu karne kaa vakt bhi jiesti ke karyanvayan se pehle kaa chunaa gaya taaki uske aane se pehle kaale dhan ke bhandar saaf ho saken
 GST and digital payments will be the two decisive elements of the monitoring and balancing mechanism we have developed in the last two years to prevent black money from being created in future
 ye saare kadam ek badlaavkaari satta parivartan kii ore ishaara karte hai jahaan sarkaar galat kaamon main lage logon ko spasht sandesh bhej rahi he

 isse aupchaarik arthvyavastha main bahi-khaataa rakhane or uskaa aakaar jaanane main madad milti he
